Finally, I chose Peacock King, which is in Qihe County and is very close to the Animal Kingdom in more than ten minutes! After booking with Ctrip, I received a call from the staff Ni Shasha one day in advance to confirm the check-in and add WeChat. Shasha warmly informed us of the location and weather temperature. After arriving, I went directly to the fourth floor to check in. We arrived at almost ten o'clock in the evening. At more than eight o'clock, Shasha also contacted us on WeChat to inform us that we had prepared good night milk for the children, and the precautions for dining and hot springs the next day. It was very thoughtful~
When checking in, I saw that I brought a child and gave him a high-legged car. I kept playing with it in my hands during the two days I played there. Haha, the child received a small gift and was very happy.
The room is large, warm, the light is slightly darker, there is a terrace, there is plenty of bottled water in the room, and there is a fruit plate. The oranges and tomatoes are delicious haha~
There are some shortcomings, the light is dim, the vision is inconvenient, the quilt is warm, the quilt cover is hard, and it will make noise when turning over. If you sleep lightly, it will have a little impact, but these do not affect my good impression of this hotel. The hygiene is dark, so it's hard to see clearly. There are double eyelids of the previous guest stuck on the big dressing mirror, and the rag that the lady forgot to take away after cleaning up... Oh, by the way, there are no disposable underwear in the hot spring, if you wear a swimsuit and don't bring it, you have to go in without anything üòÇ
The deepest feeling is the staff Ni Shasha's concern, good night milk, whether you got home safely, and if you have any questions, you will get a response quickly on WeChat, which is great! All five-star praise! I hope I will have the opportunity to stay in the future~
